aobscanmodule(INJECT_SteamData,GameAssembly.dll,83 78 64 03 0F 94 C0) // should be unique
alloc(newmem,$1000)
registersymbol(INJECT_SteamData SteamData)
label(return SteamData)

newmem:
  mov [SteamData],eax
  cmp dword ptr [eax+64],03
  jmp return

SteamData:
dq 0

INJECT_SteamData:
  jmp newmem
  nop 2
return:

//Player Loc

aobscanmodule(INJECT_PlayerCoords,UnityPlayer.dll,0F 10 43 2C 0F 11 85 28 FF FF FF) // should be unique
alloc(newmemLoc,$1000)
registersymbol(INJECT_PlayerCoords PlayerCoords)
label(returnLoc codeLoc PlayerCoords)

newmemLoc:
  cmp [ebx+68],1
  jne codeLoc
  mov [PlayerCoords],ebx
codeLoc:
  movups xmm0,[ebx+2C]
  movups [ebp-000000D8],xmm0
  jmp returnLoc

PlayerCoords:
dq 0

INJECT_PlayerCoords:
  jmp newmemLoc
  nop 6
returnLoc:

[DISABLE]

INJECT_SteamData:
  db 83 78 64 03 0F 94 C0

unregistersymbol(*)
dealloc(*)


INJECT_PlayerCoords:
  db 0F 10 43 2C 0F 11 85 28 FF FF FF

unregistersymbol(*)
dealloc(*)

[ENABLE]

aobscanmodule(INJECT_VoteTimer,GameAssembly.dll,F3 0F 10 87 A0 00 00 00 6A) // should be unique
alloc(newmem,$1000)
registersymbol(INJECT_VoteTimer SteamVote)
label(return SteamVote)

newmem:

  mov [SteamVote],edi
  movss xmm0,[edi+000000A0]
  jmp return

SteamVote:
dq 0

INJECT_VoteTimer:
  jmp newmem
  nop 3
return:

[DISABLE]

INJECT_VoteTimer:
  db F3 0F 10 87 A0 00 00 00

unregistersymbol(*)
dealloc(*)

votePlayerCount = readByte("[[SteamVote]+5C]+C")

function Addy(x)
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 1 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+10]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 2 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+14]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 3 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+18]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 4 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+1C]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 5 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+20]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 6 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+24]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 7 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+28]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 8 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+2C]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 9 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+30]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 10 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+34]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 11 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+38]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 12 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+3C]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 13 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+40]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 14 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+44]+5B",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 15 then
writeInteger("[[[SteamVote]+5C]+48]+5B",x)
end

end


[ENABLE]
local vote = {}

local playerName = readString("[[[[[SteamVote]+5C]+10]+4C]+84]+C",90,1)
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 1 then
   table.insert(vote,"  " .. playerName)
end

local playerName = readString("[[[[[SteamVote]+5C]+14]+4C]+84]+C",90,1)
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 2 then
   table.insert(vote,"  " .. playerName)
end

local file, err = io.open("vote.txt", 'w')
  for k, v in pairs(vote) do file:write (v,'\n') end
  file:close()

local file, err = io.open("vote.txt", 'r')
	if err then
		error(err)
	elseif file then
		fileStr = file:read('*all')
		file:close()
	end


local list = createStringlist()
list.Text = fileStr

os.remove("vote.txt")





local voteForce = showSelectionList('MUST BE HOST TO FORCE VOTE!', 'Pick Player To Force Vote On', list)

if voteForce == 0 then
Addy(voteForce)
 elseif voteForce == 1 then
Addy(voteForce)
  elseif voteForce == 2 then
Addy(voteForce)
  elseif voteForce == 3 then
Addy(voteForce)
  elseif voteForce == 4 then
Addy(voteForce)
  elseif voteForce == 5 then
Addy(voteForce)
  elseif voteForce == 6 then

local yOffset = '+30'
--local zOffset = '+68'

local yCoord = (teleportAddy..yOffset)
--local zCoord = (teleportAddy..zOffset)

table.insert(script, "if syntaxcheck then return end")
table.insert(script, "[ENABLE]")
table.insert(script, "")

table.insert(script, [[writeFloat(']]..yCoord..[[',]]..readFloat (yCoord)..') -- Y Coord')

table.insert(script, [[local t = createTimer()
  t.Interval,t.OnTimer = 1000,function(tm)
   tm.Destroy()
   memrec.Active = false
end]])

table.insert(script, "")
table.insert(script, "[DISABLE]")



MRLoc = AddressList.getMemoryRecordByDescription('&lt;-- Save Current Location To Table')

local mr = AddressList.createMemoryRecord()
mr.Description = [[Teleport To: ]]
mr.Type = vtAutoAssembler
mr.appendToEntry(MRLoc)
mr.Script = table.concat(script, '\n')

   tm.Destroy()
   memrec.Active = false

aobscanmodule(INJECT_GamePassClient,GameAssembly.dll,83 B9 AC 00 00 00 03) // should be unique
alloc(newmem,$1000,INJECT_GamePassClient)

label(return GamepassPlayers)

newmem:
  mov [GamepassPlayers],rcx
  cmp dword ptr [rcx+000000AC],03
  jmp return

GamepassPlayers:
dq 0

INJECT_GamePassClient:
  jmp newmem
  nop 2
return:

label(returnXboxLoc codeXboxLoc XboxPlayerCoords)

newmemXboxLoc:
  cmp [rcx+198],#1
  jne codeXboxLoc
  mov [XboxPlayerCoords],rcx

codeXboxLoc:
  movss xmm9,[rcx+30]
  jmp returnXboxLoc

XboxPlayerCoords:
dq 0

INJECT_XboxPlayerCoords:
  jmp newmemXboxLoc
returnXboxLoc:

votePlayerCount = readByte("[[XboxVote]+88]+18")

function Addy(x)
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 1 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+20]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 2 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+28]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 3 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+30]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 4 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+38]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 5 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+40]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 6 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+48]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 7 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+50]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 8 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+58]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 9 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+60]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 10 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+68]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 11 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+70]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 12 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+78]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 13 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+80]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 14 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+88]+B3",x)
end
if votePlayerCount &gt;= 15 then
writeInteger("[[[XboxVote]+88]+90]+B3",x)
end

end

table.insert(script, "[ENABLE]")
table.insert(script, "")

table.insert(script, [[writeFloat(']]..xCoord..[[',]]..readFloat (xCoord)..') -- X Coord')

table.insert(script, [[writeFloat(']]..yCoord..[[',]]..readFloat (yCoord)..') -- Y Coord')

--table.insert(script, [[writeFloat(']]..zCoord..[[',]]..readFloat (zCoord)..') -- Z Coord')

table.insert(script, "")


table.insert(script, [[local t = createTimer()
  t.Interval,t.OnTimer = 1000,function(tm)
   tm.Destroy()
   memrec.Active = false
end]])

table.insert(script, "")
table.insert(script, "[DISABLE]")



MRLoc = AddressList.getMemoryRecordByDescription('&lt;-- Save Current Location To Table (Gamepass)')

local mr = AddressList.createMemoryRecord()
mr.Description = [[Teleport To: ]]
mr.Type = vtAutoAssembler
mr.appendToEntry(MRLoc)
mr.Script = table.concat(script, '\n')



local t = createTimer()
  t.Interval,t.OnTimer = 1000,function(tm)
   tm.Destroy()
   memrec.Active = false
end

  <UserdefinedSymbols/>
  <LuaScript>----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- SET VARIABLES

--Needed Variables To Set:

--CREATE NEW MEMRECORD:
--Please Attach To Process -" ChanceToGameName "



local GameExe = "Among Us.exe"
local GameName = "Among Us"


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Custom Function Commands
--[[


-- Enable / Disable Compact Mode
compactEnable()
compactDisable()

--Disable All Scripts
disableAllScripts()

--Un X Memrecord
unX("Memrecord Name, Disable Time")   Example: unX("test", 500)

--Set Memrecord Color
setColor(Name, Color)    Example: setColor("test", green)

--AddressList.getMemoryRecordByDescription()
getDescription()
]]
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Set Color Codes
red = "0x0000FF"
green = "0x008000"
lightGreen = "0x00FF00"
blue = "0xFF0000"
magenta = "0xFF00FF"
purple = "0x800080"
darkPurple = "0x400080"
brown = "0x000080"
grey = "0x808080"
black = "0x000000"
orange = "0x0080FF"
yellow = "0x00FFFF"

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Auto Attach + Set Status

if getCEVersion() &lt; 7.2 then showMessage("Please update to Cheat Engine 7.2 or Higher")
return end

mr = AddressList.getMemoryRecordByDescription("Successfully attached to"..[[" ]]..GameName..[[ "]])

if mr ~= nil then
  mr.setDescription("Please Attach To Process -"..[[" ]]..GameName..[[ "]])
  mr.Color =0x0000FF
else
end

local mr = AddressList.getMemoryRecordByDescription("Please Attach To Process -"..[[" ]]..GameName..[[ "]])

strings_add(getAutoAttachList(), GameExe)

function onOpenProcess(processid)

  mr.setDescription("Successfully attached to"..[[" ]]..GameName..[[ "]])
  mr.Color =0x008000
end

OpenProcess(GameExe)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Compact Mode ENABLE

function compactEnable()

function cycleFullCompact(sender,force)
local state = not(compactmenuitem.Caption == 'Compact View Mode')
 if force~=nil then state = not force end
  compactmenuitem.Caption = state and 'Compact View Mode' or 'Full View Mode'
   getMainForm().Splitter1.Visible = state
   getMainForm().Panel4.Visible    = state
   getMainForm().Panel5.Visible    = state
end

function addCompactMenu()
 if compactmenualreadyexists then return
end

local parent = getMainForm().Menu.Items
 compactmenuitem = createMenuItem(parent)
 parent.add(compactmenuitem)
 compactmenuitem.Caption = 'Compact View Mode'
 compactmenuitem.OnClick = cycleFullCompact
 compactmenualreadyexists = 'yes'
end

addCompactMenu()
cycleFullCompact(nil,true)

end

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Compact Mode DISABLE

function compactDisable()

cycleFullCompact(nil,false)

end

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Disable All Scripts

function disableAllScripts()

local mainHook = ('Among Us')
local al = getAddressList()
for i = 0, al.Count - 1 do
    if al[i].Active == true and al[i].Description ~= mainHook then al[i].Active = false
 end
end
for i = 0, al.Count - 1 do
     if al[i].Active == true  then al[i].Active = false
 end
end

end

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
--Un X Memrecord

function unX(var1, var2)
local mrDisable = AddressList.getMemoryRecordByDescription(var1)
   local t = createTimer()
   t.Interval,t.OnTimer = var2,function(tm)
     tm.Destroy()
     mrDisable.Active = false
   end

end


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
--Memrecord Set Color

function setColor(var1, var2)

local colorSet = AddressList.getMemoryRecordByDescription(var1)
      colorSet.Color = var2

end

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
--memrecord by description
getDescription = AddressList.getMemoryRecordByDescription


</LuaScript>
</CheatTable>
